          float2 tc0        : TEXCOORD0,
          float2 tc1        : TEXCOORD1,
          out float4 ocolor : COLOR)

  color = color * cxmul + cxadd;
  color = lerp (1, color, color.a);
  ocolor.rgb = color * color.a;
  ocolor.a = color.a;
